It&#39;d take a lot of work to restore the once magnificent creation to it&#39;s former glory,  but it wasn&#39;t a task that couldn&#39;t be accomplished with some hard work. The girl quickly left the scene to go to the nearest hardware store.

After a small while she returned with a wheel barrow carrying several bags of concrete. One at a time she plopped the bags onto the ground at the entrance to the bridge.

After she emptied her cart she returned to th store to get more.

<br><font size=-3><font color = white><font color=#666699>Rather than assisting with the reconstruction of the bridge above-ground, Saigosame opted to take another approach. With the damage to the bridge, it was possible that the support struts of the bridge had been damaged, and even if the bridge itself was repaired, if the supports were left unobserved it could be possible that the bridge would simply crumble once more upon being repaired. As such, the Hoshigaki dove from the bridge&#39;s damaged form into the waters below, utilizing his aptitude for the water to properly observe the support struts that connected the bridge to the water&#39;s floor.

He remained underneath the water for some time, his form circling the northern points of the bridge as he looked over the concrete support struts closest to the the Village... And thankfully, there were no issues. But moving further south, where the damage was the worst, there were some glaring issues in the concrete. Cracks, where the explosion had damaged the supports, exposing the core of the concrete to the elements - And more importantly, the water.

He brought himself back up from the water&#39;s depths, shouting back up to the bridge.
<font color = white>&#34;There&#39;s a MASSIVE crack here on the supports, it needs more concrete to fill it!&#34;</font>, he yelled, before tossing up a reel of what appeared to be kelp to the bridge, essentially marking the location of the damaged support.<br>(<a href=?src=[0x3000037];action=name;character=f53986565ecee36cbb0359fd26fa7a6fc13f161c9841fb578b884e812d03e0ff style = "text-decoration: none; color: #666699;">The shark-like boy</a>)</font></font></font>
